    window.Riot = window.Riot || {};

    if (!Riot.getCookie) {
        Riot.getCookie = function getCookie(cookie) {
            cookie = encodeURIComponent(cookie);
            var regex = new RegExp(cookie + '=([^;]*)'),
                    match = regex.exec(document.cookie);

            if (match) {
                return decodeURIComponent(match[1]);
            }

            return false;
        };
    }

    Riot.setup = function () {
        if (window.Codex && Codex.setup) {
            Codex.setup();
        } else {
            setTimeout(Riot.setup, 100);
        }
    }
</script>
